[30;1m59 | [0m[35mserial port otherwise it could block forever if no newline character is[0m
[30;1m60 | [0m[35mreceived. Also note that :meth:`readlines` only works with a timeout.[0m
[30;1m61 | [0m[35m:meth:`readlines` depends on having a timeout and interprets that as EOF (end[0m
